# 13 - сообщение что продать флот не удалось
# 70 - ежемесячная проверка наличия флота на продаже
# 71 - проверка наличия энергокредитов
# 72 - проверка необходимости покупки
# 80 - ежегодная проверка условий продажи для ии
# 81 - выставление флота на продажу (ИИ)
# 98 - сообщение-уведомление о том что нашу ставку сбили
# 99 - сообщение-уведомление

# 901 - окно дипломатии с Аукционом
# 999 - проверка на геноцидоидальность

							is_ship_class = shipclass_habitat_station
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							has_fleet_flag = armada_of_the_voidborn
							has_fleet_flag = star_rider_flotilla
							has_fleet_flag = first_storm_wing
							has_fleet_flag = dwamak_bashers
							has_fleet_flag = unhinged_screamer_flotilla
							has_fleet_flag = frenzied_volunteer_squadron
							has_fleet_flag = her_chosen_champions
							has_fleet_flag = order_of_eternal_night
							has_fleet_flag = twilight_congregation
							has_fleet_flag = ftm_rented_fleet_slot_1
							has_fleet_flag = ftm_rented_fleet_slot_2
							has_fleet_flag = ftm_rented_fleet_slot_3
							has_fleet_flag = ftm_rented_fleet_slot_4
							has_fleet_flag = ftm_rented_fleet_slot_5
							has_fleet_flag = ftm_rented_fleet_slot_6
						}
					}
				}
				save_event_target_as = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_05
				solar_system = {
					space_owner = {
						save_event_target_as = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_05_buyer
					}
				}
			}
		}
		save_global_event_target_as = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller
		log = "[Root.GetName] запустил аукцион флота"
		set_variable = {
			which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_cost_manual
			value = 100
		}
	}
		
	# выбор флота 1
	option = {
		name = ftm_auction.101.fleet_01
		custom_tooltip = ftm_auction.101.fleet_01.tooltip
		trigger = {
			exists = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_01 
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			log = "[Root.GetName] выбрал для аукциона флот 1 ([event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_01.GetFleetName])"
			event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_01 = { 
				save_global_event_target_as = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1
			}
			country_event = { id = ftm_auction.102 }
		}
	}
		
	# выбор флота 2
	option = {
		name = ftm_auction.101.fleet_02
		custom_tooltip = ftm_auction.101.fleet_02.tooltip
		trigger = {
			exists = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_02
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			log = "[Root.GetName] выбрал для аукциона флот 2 ([event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_02.GetFleetName])"
			event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_02 = { 
				save_global_event_target_as = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1
			}
			country_event = { id = ftm_auction.102 }
		}
	}
		
	# выбор флота 3
	option = {
		name = ftm_auction.101.fleet_03
		custom_tooltip = ftm_auction.101.fleet_03.tooltip
		trigger = {
			exists = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_03
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			log = "[Root.GetName] выбрал для аукциона флот 3 ([event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_03.GetFleetName])"
			event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_03 = { 
				save_global_event_target_as = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1
			}
			country_event = { id = ftm_auction.102 }
		}
	}
		
	# выбор флота 4
	option = {
		name = ftm_auction.101.fleet_04
		custom_tooltip = ftm_auction.101.fleet_04.tooltip
		trigger = {
			exists = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_04
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			log = "[Root.GetName] выбрал для аукциона флот 4 ([event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_04.GetFleetName])"
			event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_04 = { 
				save_global_event_target_as = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1
			}
			country_event = { id = ftm_auction.102 }
		}
	}
		
	# выбор флота 5
	option = {
		name = ftm_auction.101.fleet_05
		custom_tooltip = ftm_auction.101.fleet_05.tooltip
		trigger = {
			exists = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_05

	}
		
	# передумал

		hidden_effect = {
			log = "[Root.GetName] выбрал передумал продавать флот"
			remove_global_flag = ftm_auction_lot_1_in_progress	
		}
	}

# 2 - ручная настройка стартовой цены аукциона
country_event = {
	id = ftm_auction.102
	title = "ftm_auction.102.title"
	desc = "ftm_auction.102.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_federation_fleet 
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	# -10000
	option = {
		name = ftm_auction.102.minus10000
		custom_tooltip = ftm_auction.102.minus10000.tooltip
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_cost_manual
				value >= 10001
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			change_variable = {
				which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_cost_manual
				value = -10000
			}
			country_event = { id = ftm_auction.102 }
			log = "[event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller.GetName] снижает цену на 10000 единиц. Текущая цена: [Root.ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_cost_manual]"
		}
	}

				value = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_cost_manual

				which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_cost_plus_10000
				value = 10000

			log = "[Root.GetName] выставляет флот [event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1.GetFleetName] на аукцион за стартовую цену: [Root.ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_cost]. Нужно подтверждение"
		}
	}

# 3 - запрос подтверждения продажи
country_event = {
	id = ftm_auction.103
	title = "ftm_auction.103.title"
	desc = "ftm_auction.103.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_federation_fleet 
	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1
		
	# подтвердить
	option = {
		name = ftm_auction.103.confirm
		custom_tooltip = ftm_auction.103.confirm.tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			log = "[Root.GetName] подтверждает продажу флота [event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1.GetFleetName] через аукцион"
			country_event = { id = ftm_auction.104 }
			remove_global_flag = ftm_auction_lot_1_in_progress
			set_global_flag = ftm_auction_lot_1_selected
			event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1 = { 
				set_owner = event_target:ftm_auction_country
				set_event_locked = yes
				fleet_event = { id = ftm_auction.199 }
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = ftm_auction_lot_1_time_in_months
				value = 24
			}
		}
	}
		
	# отказаться
	option = {
		name = ftm_auction.103.nope
		hidden_effect = {
			log = "[Root.GetName] выбрал передумал выставлять флот [event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1.GetFleetName] на аукцион"
			remove_global_flag = ftm_auction_lot_1_in_progress	
		}
	}
	
}





# 4 - выставление на аукцион
country_event = {
	id = ftm_auction.104
	hide_window = yes	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
	
		# ОБНУЛЕНИЕ СЧЕТЧИКОВ
		event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
			# корветы (corvette)
			set_variable = {
				which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_corvette_count # всего
				value = 0
			}
			# эсминцы (destroyer)
			set_variable = {
				which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_destroyer_count # всего
				value = 0
			}
			# крейсера (cruiser)
			set_variable = {
				which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_cruiser_count # всего
				value = 0
			}
			# линкоры (battleship)
			set_variable = {
				which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_battleship_count # всего
				value = 0
			}
			# титаны (titan)
			set_variable = {
				which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_titan_count # всего
				value = 0
			}
		}
		
		# ПРИСВОЕНИЕ СЧЕТЧИКОВ		
		
		# корветы (corvette)
		every_owned_ship = {
			limit = {
				ftm_corvette_ship_size_types = yes
				fleet = {
					is_same_value = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1 
				}
			}	
			event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
				change_variable = {
					which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_corvette_count # всего
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
			
		# эсминцы (destroyer)
		every_owned_ship = {
			limit = {
				ftm_destroyer_ship_size_types = yes
				fleet = {
					is_same_value = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1 
				}
			}
			event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
				change_variable = {
					which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_destroyer_count # всего
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
			
		# крейсера (cruiser)
		every_owned_ship = {
			limit = {
				ftm_cruiser_ship_size_types = yes
				fleet = {
					is_same_value = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1 
				}
			}
			event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
				change_variable = {
					which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_cruiser_count # всего
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
			
		# линкоры (battleship)
		every_owned_ship = {
			limit = {
				ftm_battleship_ship_size_types = yes
				fleet = {
					is_same_value = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1 
				}
				
			}
			event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
				change_variable = {
					which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_battleship_count # всего
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
			
		# титаны (titan)
		every_owned_ship = {
			limit = {
				ftm_titan_ship_size_types = yes
				fleet = {
					is_same_value = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1 
				}
			}
			event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = {
				change_variable = {
					which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_titan_count # всего
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# 9 - обратный отсчет счетчика времени лота
event = {
	id = ftm_auction.109
	hide_window = yes	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_global_flag = ftm_auction_lot_1_selected
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
					check_variable = {
						which = ftm_auction_lot_1_time_in_months
						value >= 1
					}
				}
			}
			event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
				change_variable = {
					which = ftm_auction_lot_1_time_in_months
					value = -1
				}
			}
			log = "Лот активен. Осталось месяцев: [event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller.ftm_auction_lot_1_time_in_months]"
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						exists = event_target:ftm_auction_lot_1_max_price
					}
					event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
						check_variable = {
							which = ftm_auction_lot_1_time_in_months
							value < 1
						}
					}
				}
			}
			log = "Лот не был куплен. Возврат флота..."
			event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1 = { 
				set_owner = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller
				set_event_locked = no
			}
			event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
				country_event = { id = ftm_auction.113 }
			}
			remove_global_flag = ftm_auction_lot_1_selected
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					exists = event_target:ftm_auction_lot_1_max_price
					event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
						check_variable = {
							which = ftm_auction_lot_1_time_in_months
							value < 1
						}
					}
				}
			}
			log = "Лот куплен империей [event_target:ftm_auction_lot_1_max_price.GetName]. Передача флота и денег..."
			event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1 = { 
				set_owner = event_target:ftm_auction_lot_1_max_price
				set_event_locked = no
			}
			event_target:ftm_auction_lot_1_max_price = { 
				country_event = { id = ftm_auction.111 }
			}
			event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
				country_event = { id = ftm_auction.112 }
			}
			remove_global_flag = ftm_auction_lot_1_selected	
		}
	}
}

# 11 - сообщение с информацией о победе в аукционе
country_event = {
	id = ftm_auction.111
	title = "ftm_auction.111.title"
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				ftm_comparible_mods_flags = yes
			}
		}
		text = "ftm_auction.111.desc"
	}
	# mods
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			ftm_comparible_mods_flags = yes
		}
		text = "ftm_auction.111.desc_mod"
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_signing 
	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = yes
			}
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = ftm_ai_sell_block_time days = 1800 }
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = ftm_ai_buy_block_time days = 450 }
		}
	}
		
	# ок
	option = {
		name = ftm_auction.111.ok
	}
}





# 12 - сообщение с информацией об успешной продаже флота на аукционе (+ начисление денег продавцу)
country_event = {
	id = ftm_auction.112
	title = "ftm_auction.112.title"
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				ftm_comparible_mods_flags = yes
			}
		}
		text = "ftm_auction.112.desc"
	}
	# mods
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			ftm_comparible_mods_flags = yes
		}
		text = "ftm_auction.112.desc_mod"
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_signing 
	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1
	
	# ок
	option = {
		name = ftm_auction.112.ok
		custom_tooltip = ftm_auction.112.ok.tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			clear_global_event_target = ftm_auction_lot_1_max_price

			# присвоение денег продавцу
				
			event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 							
				set_variable = {
					which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_final_cost
					value = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_cost
				}
			}
			log = "[event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller.GetName]: победила цена в [event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller.ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_cost] энергии. Присвоение денег..."
			while = {
				count = 99
				if = {
					limit = {
						event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
							check_variable = {
								which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_final_cost
								value >= 10000
							}
						}
					}
					add_resource = { energy = 10000 }
					event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
						change_variable = {
							which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_final_cost
							value = -10000
						}
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
							check_variable = {
								which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_final_cost
								value >= 1000
							}
						}
					}
					add_resource = { energy = 1000 }
					event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
						change_variable = {
							which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_final_cost
							value = -1000
						}		
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
							check_variable = {
								which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_final_cost
								value >= 100
							}
						}
					}
					add_resource = { energy = 100 }
					event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
						change_variable = {
							which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_final_cost
							value = -100
						}
					}					
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
							check_variable = {
								which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_final_cost
								value >= 10
							}
						}
					}
					add_resource = { energy = 10 }
					event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
						change_variable = {
							which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_final_cost
							value = -10
						}
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
							check_variable = {
								which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_final_cost
								value >= 1
							}
						}
					}
					add_resource = { energy = 1 }
					event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
						change_variable = {
							which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_final_cost
							value = -1
						}					
					}
				}
				else = {
					#nothing
				}
			}	
			log = "[event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller.GetName]: Присвоение денег завершено"	
		
		}
	}
}

# 70 - ежемесячная проверка наличия флота на аукционе
event = {
	id = ftm_auction.170
	hide_window = yes	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_global_flag = ftm_auction_lot_1_selected
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = ftm_auction_not_can_use_ai_buy
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = ftm_auction_lot_1_selected
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = ftm_ai_buy_block_time
					}
					is_ai = yes
					is_country_type = default
					used_naval_capacity_percent < 0.8
					has_monthly_income = { resource = energy value >= 10 }
					has_monthly_income = { resource = alloys value >= 5 }
					has_communications = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller
					NOT = {
						is_same_value = event_target:ftm_auction_lot_1_max_price
					}
					NOT = {
						is_same_value = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller
					}
					NOT = {
						event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = {
							OR = {
								is_rival = prev
								opinion = {
									who = prev
									value < -50
								}
								their_opinion = {
									who = prev
									value < -50
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				random_list = {
					10 = {
						country_event = { id = ftm_auction.171 days = 1 }
					}
					10 = {
						country_event = { id = ftm_auction.171 days = 4 }
					}
					10 = {
						country_event = { id = ftm_auction.171 days = 7 }
					}
					10 = {
						country_event = { id = ftm_auction.171 days = 10 }
					}
					10 = {
						country_event = { id = ftm_auction.171 days = 13 }
					}
					10 = {
						country_event = { id = ftm_auction.171 days = 16 }
					}
					10 = {
						country_event = { id = ftm_auction.171 days = 19 }
					}
					10 = {
						country_event = { id = ftm_auction.171 days = 22 }
					}
					10 = {
						country_event = { id = ftm_auction.171 days = 25 }
					}
					10 = {
						country_event = { id = ftm_auction.171 days = 28 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}


# 71 - проверка наличия энергокредитов
country_event = {
	id = ftm_auction.171
	hide_window = yes	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_global_flag = ftm_auction_lot_1_selected
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = ftm_ai_buy_block_time
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[Root.GetName]: Запуск скрипта проверки наличия энергокредитов"
		event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
			set_variable = {
				which = ftm_buyer_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_energy_ai_current_count
				value = 0
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			which = ftm_buyer_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_energy_ai_current_count
			value = 0
		}
		save_event_target_as = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_checker
		export_resource_stockpile_to_variable = { resource = energy variable = ftm_buyer_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_energy_ai_current_count }
		event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = {
			set_variable = {
				which = ftm_buyer_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_energy_ai_current_count
				value = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_checker.ftm_buyer_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_energy_ai_current_count
			}
		}
		log = "[Root.GetName]: ЗАВЕРШЕНА ПРОВЕРКА ЭНЕРГИИ ДЛЯ ВХОДА НА АУКЦИОН. КОЛИЧЕСТВО: [event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller.ftm_buyer_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_energy_ai_current_count]."
		
		# проверка наличия энергии для входа на аукцион
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
					check_variable = {
						which = ftm_buyer_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_energy_ai_current_count
						value >= ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_cost_plus_100
					}
				}
			}
			log = "[Root.GetName]: средств для входа на аукцион достаточно."
			country_event = { id = ftm_auction.172 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
					check_variable = {
						which = ftm_buyer_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_energy_ai_current_count
						value < ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_cost_plus_100
					}
				}
			}
			log = "[Root.GetName]: не хватает средств для входа на аукцион."
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = ftm_ai_buy_block_time days = 40 }
		}
	}
}


# 72 - проверка необходимости покупки
country_event = {
	id = ftm_auction.172
	hide_window = yes	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = { # нормальные условия
						OR = {
							AND = {
								event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1 = {
									fleet_power < 2000
								}
								has_monthly_income = { resource = energy value >= 25 }
								has_monthly_income = { resource = alloys value >= 10 }
								event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
									check_variable = {
										which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_cost_plus_100
										value <= 2500
									}
								}
							}
							AND = {
								event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1 = {
									fleet_power >= 2000
									fleet_power < 5000
								}
								has_monthly_income = { resource = energy value >= 40 }
								has_monthly_income = { resource = alloys value >= 20 }

									check_variable = {

								event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1 = {
									fleet_power >= 25000
									fleet_power < 50000
								}
								has_monthly_income = { resource = energy value >= 35 }
								has_monthly_income = { resource = alloys value >= 20 }
								event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
									check_variable = {
										which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_cost_plus_100
										value <= 71600
									}
								}
							}
							AND = {
								event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1 = {
									fleet_power >= 50000
									fleet_power < 100000
								}
								has_monthly_income = { resource = energy value >= 50 }
								has_monthly_income = { resource = alloys value >= 25 }
								event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
									check_variable = {
										which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_cost_plus_100
										value <= 128600
									}
								}
							}
							AND = {
								event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1 = {
									fleet_power >= 100000
									fleet_power < 250000
								}
								has_monthly_income = { resource = energy value >= 75 }
								has_monthly_income = { resource = alloys value >= 35 }
								event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
									check_variable = {
										which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_cost_plus_100
										value <= 285800
									}
								}
							}
							AND = {
								event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1 = {
									fleet_power >= 250000
								}
								has_monthly_income = { resource = energy value >= 100 }
								has_monthly_income = { resource = alloys value >= 50 }
								event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
									check_variable = {
										which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_cost_plus_100
										value <= 500000
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			} # конец проверки
			
			log = "[Root.GetName]: делает ставку на аукционе флота."
						
			#возврат ресурсов при перебивании цены
			
			event_target:ftm_auction_lot_1_max_price = { 	
				save_event_target_as = ftm_auction_lot_1_last_price							
				event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
					set_variable = {
						which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_returned_cost
						value = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_cost
					}
				}
				log = "[Root.GetName]: [event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller.ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_returned_cost] energy received, LOT-1 has new owner. Old - [event_target:ftm_auction_lot_1_max_price.GetName]"
				while = {
					count = 99
					if = {
						limit = {
							event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
								check_variable = {
									which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_returned_cost
									value >= 10000
								}
							}
						}
						add_resource = { energy = 10000 }
						event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
							change_variable = {
								which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_returned_cost
								value = -10000
							}
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
								check_variable = {
									which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_returned_cost
									value >= 1000
								}
							}
						}
						add_resource = { energy = 1000 }
						event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
							change_variable = {
								which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_returned_cost
								value = -1000
							}		
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
								check_variable = {
									which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_returned_cost
									value >= 100
								}
							}
						}
						add_resource = { energy = 100 }
						event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
							change_variable = {
								which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_returned_cost
								value = -100
							}
						}					
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
								check_variable = {
									which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_returned_cost
									value >= 10
								}
							}
						}
						add_resource = { energy = 10 }
						event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
							change_variable = {
								which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_returned_cost
								value = -10
							}
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
								check_variable = {
									which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_returned_cost
									value >= 1
								}
							}
						}
						add_resource = { energy = 1 }
						event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
							change_variable = {
								which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_returned_cost
								value = -1
							}					
						}
					}
					else = {
						#nothing
					}
				}			
			}
			event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
				change_variable = {
					which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_cost
					value = 100
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_cost_plus_100
					value = 100
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_cost_plus_1000
					value = 100
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_cost_plus_10000
					value = 100
				}
			}				
			save_global_event_target_as = ftm_auction_lot_1_max_price
			
			
			# снятие ресурсов при установке цены				
		
			event_target:ftm_auction_lot_1_max_price = { 
				event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
					set_variable = {
						which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_lot_cost
						value = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_cost
					}
				}
				log = "[Root.GetName]: [event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller.ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_lot_cost] energy is LOT-1 cost"	
				while = {
					count = 99
					if = {
						limit = {
							event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
								check_variable = {
									which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_lot_cost
									value >= 10000
								}
							}
						}
						add_resource = { energy = -10000 }
						event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
							change_variable = {
								which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_lot_cost
								value = -10000
							}
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
								check_variable = {
									which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_lot_cost
									value >= 1000
								}
							}
						}
						add_resource = { energy = -1000 }
						event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
							change_variable = {
								which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_lot_cost
								value = -1000
							}		
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
								check_variable = {
									which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_lot_cost
									value >= 100
								}
							}
						}
						add_resource = { energy = -100 }
						event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
							change_variable = {
								which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_lot_cost
								value = -100
							}
						}					
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
								check_variable = {
									which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_lot_cost
									value >= 10
								}
							}
						}
						add_resource = { energy = -10 }
						event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
							change_variable = {
								which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_lot_cost
								value = -10
							}
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
								check_variable = {
									which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_lot_cost
									value >= 1
								}
							}
						}
						add_resource = { energy = -1 }
						event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = { 
							change_variable = {
								which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_lot_cost
								value = -1
							}					
						}
					}
					else = {
						#nothing
					}
				}	
			}
			event_target:ftm_auction_lot_1_last_price = {
				country_event = { id = ftm_auction.198 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = ftm_ai_buy_block_time days = 300 }
		}
	}
}



# 80 - ежегодная проверка условий продажи для ии
event = {
	id = ftm_auction.180
	hide_window = yes	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = ftm_auction_lot_1_selected
				has_global_flag = ftm_auction_lot_1_in_progress	
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = ftm_auction_not_can_use_ai_sale
		}
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = crisis_stage_1
				has_global_flag = crisis_stage_2
				has_global_flag = crisis_stage_3
				has_global_flag = crisis_stage_4
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = gray_goo_crisis_active
					NOT = {
						has_global_flag = graygoo_defeated
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = marauder_crisis_started
					NOT = {
						has_global_flag = great_khan_dead
					}
				}
				has_global_flag = war_in_heaven_ongoing
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = ftm_auction_lot_1_selected
						has_global_flag = ftm_auction_lot_1_in_progress	
					}
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = ftm_ai_sell_block_time
					}
					is_homicidal = no
					is_ai = yes
					is_country_type = default
					is_at_war = no
					used_naval_capacity_percent > 0.8
					resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value < 50000 }
					NOT = {
						any_neighbor_country = {
							is_country_type = default
							OR = {
								is_homicidal = yes
								is_rival = prev
								opinion = {
									who = prev
									value < -50
								}
								their_opinion = {
									who = prev
									value < -50
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = ftm_auction_lot_1_num_fleet_count
					value = 0
				}
				every_owned_fleet = {
					limit = {
						fleet_power > 2000
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								is_ship_class = shipclass_constructor
								is_ship_class = shipclass_colonizer
								is_ship_class = shipclass_science_ship
								is_ship_class = shipclass_transport
								is_ship_class = shipclass_starbase
								is_ship_class = shipclass_military_special
								is_ship_class = shipclass_military_station
								is_ship_class = shipclass_mining_station
								is_ship_class = shipclass_research_station
								is_ship_class = shipclass_observation_station
								is_ship_class = shipclass_habitat_station
							}
						}
					}
					owner = {
						change_variable = {
							which = ftm_auction_lot_1_num_fleet_count
							value = 1
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							which = ftm_auction_lot_1_num_fleet_count
							value > 2
						}
					}
					random_list = {
						10 = {
							country_event = { id = ftm_auction.181 days = 5 }
						}
						10 = {
							country_event = { id = ftm_auction.181 days = 35 }
						}
						10 = {
							country_event = { id = ftm_auction.181 days = 65 }
						}
						10 = {
							country_event = { id = ftm_auction.181 days = 95 }
						}
						10 = {
							country_event = { id = ftm_auction.181 days = 125 }
						}
						10 = {
							country_event = { id = ftm_auction.181 days = 155 }
						}
						10 = {
							country_event = { id = ftm_auction.181 days = 185 }
						}
						10 = {
							country_event = { id = ftm_auction.181 days = 215 }
						}
						10 = {
							country_event = { id = ftm_auction.181 days = 245 }
						}
						10 = {
							country_event = { id = ftm_auction.181 days = 275 }
						}
						10 = {
							country_event = { id = ftm_auction.181 days = 305 }
						}
						10 = {
							country_event = { id = ftm_auction.181 days = 335 }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}


# 81 - выставление флота на продажу (ИИ)
country_event = {
	id = ftm_auction.181
	hide_window = yes	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = ftm_auction_lot_1_selected
				has_global_flag = ftm_auction_lot_1_in_progress	
				has_country_flag = ftm_ai_sell_block_time
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		save_global_event_target_as = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_owned_fleet = {
					AND = {
						is_alliance_fleet = no
						solar_system = {
							exists = space_owner
							space_owner = {
								is_same_value = root
							}
						}
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								is_ship_class = shipclass_constructor
								is_ship_class = shipclass_colonizer
								is_ship_class = shipclass_science_ship
								is_ship_class = shipclass_transport
								is_ship_class = shipclass_starbase
								is_ship_class = shipclass_military_special
								is_ship_class = shipclass_military_station
								is_ship_class = shipclass_mining_station
								is_ship_class = shipclass_research_station
								is_ship_class = shipclass_observation_station
								is_ship_class = shipclass_habitat_station
							}
						}
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								has_fleet_flag = armada_of_the_voidborn
								has_fleet_flag = star_rider_flotilla
								has_fleet_flag = first_storm_wing
								has_fleet_flag = dwamak_bashers
								has_fleet_flag = unhinged_screamer_flotilla
								has_fleet_flag = frenzied_volunteer_squadron
								has_fleet_flag = her_chosen_champions
								has_fleet_flag = order_of_eternal_night
								has_fleet_flag = twilight_congregation
								has_fleet_flag = ftm_rented_fleet_lot_1
								has_fleet_flag = ftm_rented_fleet_lot_1
								has_fleet_flag = ftm_rented_fleet_lot_3
								has_fleet_flag = ftm_rented_fleet_lot_4
								has_fleet_flag = ftm_rented_fleet_lot_5
								has_fleet_flag = ftm_rented_fleet_lot_6
							}
						}
						OR = {
							AND = {
								fleet_power > 2000
								years_passed >= 20
								years_passed < 50
							}
							AND = {
								fleet_power > 5000
								years_passed >= 50
								years_passed < 100
							}
							AND = {
								fleet_power > 10000
								years_passed >= 100
								years_passed < 150
							}
							AND = {
								fleet_power > 20000
								years_passed >= 150
								years_passed < 200
							}
							AND = {
								fleet_power > 30000
								years_passed >= 200
							}
							AND = {
								fleet_power > 10000
								mid_game_years_passed > 0
							}
							AND = {
								fleet_power > 30000
								end_game_years_passed > 0
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			random_owned_fleet = {
				limit = {
					is_alliance_fleet = no
					solar_system = {
						exists = space_owner
						space_owner = {
							is_same_value = root
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							is_ship_class = shipclass_constructor
							is_ship_class = shipclass_colonizer
							is_ship_class = shipclass_science_ship
							is_ship_class = shipclass_transport
							is_ship_class = shipclass_starbase
							is_ship_class = shipclass_military_special
							is_ship_class = shipclass_military_station
							is_ship_class = shipclass_mining_station
							is_ship_class = shipclass_research_station
							is_ship_class = shipclass_observation_station
							is_ship_class = shipclass_habitat_station
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							has_fleet_flag = armada_of_the_voidborn
							has_fleet_flag = star_rider_flotilla
							has_fleet_flag = first_storm_wing
							has_fleet_flag = dwamak_bashers
							has_fleet_flag = unhinged_screamer_flotilla
							has_fleet_flag = frenzied_volunteer_squadron
							has_fleet_flag = her_chosen_champions
							has_fleet_flag = order_of_eternal_night
							has_fleet_flag = twilight_congregation
							has_fleet_flag = ftm_rented_fleet_lot_1
							has_fleet_flag = ftm_rented_fleet_lot_1
							has_fleet_flag = ftm_rented_fleet_lot_3
							has_fleet_flag = ftm_rented_fleet_lot_4
							has_fleet_flag = ftm_rented_fleet_lot_5
							has_fleet_flag = ftm_rented_fleet_lot_6
						}
					}
					OR = {
						AND = {
							fleet_power > 2000
							years_passed >= 20
							years_passed < 50
						}
						AND = {
							fleet_power > 5000
							years_passed >= 50
							years_passed < 100
						}
						AND = {
							fleet_power > 10000
							years_passed >= 100
							years_passed < 150
						}
						AND = {
							fleet_power > 20000
							years_passed >= 150
							years_passed < 200
						}
						AND = {
							fleet_power > 30000
							years_passed >= 200
						}
						AND = {
							fleet_power > 10000
							mid_game_years_passed > 0
						}
						AND = {
							fleet_power > 30000
							end_game_years_passed > 0
						}
					}
				}
				save_global_event_target_as = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1
				log = "[Root.GetName] выбрал для аукциона флот 1 ([event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1.GetFleetName])"
				event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = {
					set_variable = {
						which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_cost
						value = 0
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						fleet_power < 3000
					}
					event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller = {
						change_variable = {
							which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_cost
							value = 1500
						}
						while = {
							count = 9
							random_list = {
								10 = {
									modifier = {
										factor = 0
										check_variable = {
											which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_cost
											value < 1200
										}
									}
									multiply_variable = {
										which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_cost
										value = 0.9
									}
								}
								10 = {
									modifier = {
										factor = 0
										check_variable = {
											which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_cost
											value < 1200
										}
									}
									multiply_variable = {
										which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_cost
										value = 0.92
									}
								}
								10 = {
									modifier = {
										factor = 0
										check_variable = {
											which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_cost
											value < 1200
										}
									}
									multiply_variable = {
										which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_cost
										value = 0.95
									}
								}
								10 = {
									modifier = {
										factor = 0
										check_variable = {
											which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_cost
											value < 1200
										}
									}
									multiply_variable = {
										which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_cost
										value = 0.97
									}
								}
								10 = {
									modifier = {
										factor = 0
										check_variable = {
											which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_cost
											value < 1200
										}
									}
									multiply_variable = {
										which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_cost
										value = 0.99

	id = ftm_auction.198
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		create_message = {
			type = FTM_AUCTION_LOT_LOST
			localization = FTM_AUCTION_LOT_1_PRICE_LOST
			days = 30
			target = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1
			variable = {
				type = name
				localization = COUNTRY
				scope = event_target:ftm_auction_lot_1_max_price
			}
			variable = {
				type = name
				localization = FLEET
				scope = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1
			}
		}
	}		
}



# 99 - сообщение-уведомление
fleet_event = {
	id = ftm_auction.199
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		every_country = {
			limit = { 
				AND = {
					is_country_type = default 
					has_communications = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller
					is_homicidal = no
				}
			}
			create_message = {
				type = FTM_MESSAGE
				localization = FTM_AUCTION_LOT_1_NOTIFICATION
				days = 30
				target = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1
				variable = {
					type = name
					localization = COUNTRY
					scope = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1_seller
				}
				variable = {
					type = name
					localization = FLEET
					scope = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_1
				}
			}
		}
	}		
}

						}

				}
				save_event_target_as = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_03
				solar_system = {
					space_owner = {
						save_event_target_as = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_03_buyer
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_owned_fleet = {
					AND = {
						NOT = {
							exists = leader
						}
						is_alliance_fleet = no
						solar_system = {
							exists = space_owner
							space_owner = {
								is_country = ROOT
							}
						}
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								is_same_value = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_01 
								is_same_value = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_02 
								is_same_value = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_03
							}
						}
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								is_ship_class = shipclass_constructor
								is_ship_class = shipclass_colonizer
								is_ship_class = shipclass_science_ship
								is_ship_class = shipclass_transport
								is_ship_class = shipclass_starbase
								is_ship_class = shipclass_military_special
								is_ship_class = shipclass_military_station
								is_ship_class = shipclass_mining_station
								is_ship_class = shipclass_research_station
								is_ship_class = shipclass_observation_station
								is_ship_class = shipclass_habitat_station
							}
						}
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								has_fleet_flag = armada_of_the_voidborn
								has_fleet_flag = star_rider_flotilla
								has_fleet_flag = first_storm_wing
								has_fleet_flag = dwamak_bashers
								has_fleet_flag = unhinged_screamer_flotilla
								has_fleet_flag = frenzied_volunteer_squadron
								has_fleet_flag = her_chosen_champions
								has_fleet_flag = order_of_eternal_night
								has_fleet_flag = twilight_congregation
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			random_owned_fleet = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						exists = leader
					}
					is_alliance_fleet = no
					solar_system = {
						exists = space_owner
						space_owner = {
							is_country = ROOT
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							is_same_value = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_01 
							is_same_value = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_02 
							is_same_value = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_03
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							is_ship_class = shipclass_constructor
							is_ship_class = shipclass_colonizer
							is_ship_class = shipclass_science_ship
							is_ship_class = shipclass_transport
							is_ship_class = shipclass_starbase
							is_ship_class = shipclass_military_special
							is_ship_class = shipclass_military_station
							is_ship_class = shipclass_mining_station
							is_ship_class = shipclass_research_station
							is_ship_class = shipclass_observation_station
							is_ship_class = shipclass_habitat_station
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							has_fleet_flag = armada_of_the_voidborn
							has_fleet_flag = star_rider_flotilla
							has_fleet_flag = first_storm_wing
							has_fleet_flag = dwamak_bashers
							has_fleet_flag = unhinged_screamer_flotilla
							has_fleet_flag = frenzied_volunteer_squadron
							has_fleet_flag = her_chosen_champions
							has_fleet_flag = order_of_eternal_night
							has_fleet_flag = twilight_congregation
						}
					}
				}
				save_event_target_as = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_04
				solar_system = {
					space_owner = {
						save_event_target_as = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_04_buyer
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_owned_fleet = {
					AND = {
						NOT = {
							exists = leader
						}
						is_alliance_fleet = no
						solar_system = {
							exists = space_owner
							space_owner = {
								is_country = ROOT
							}
						}
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								is_same_value = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_01 
								is_same_value = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_02 
								is_same_value = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_03
								is_same_value = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_04
							}
						}
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								is_ship_class = shipclass_constructor
								is_ship_class = shipclass_colonizer
								is_ship_class = shipclass_science_ship
								is_ship_class = shipclass_transport
								is_ship_class = shipclass_starbase
								is_ship_class = shipclass_military_special
								is_ship_class = shipclass_military_station
								is_ship_class = shipclass_mining_station
								is_ship_class = shipclass_research_station
								is_ship_class = shipclass_observation_station
								is_ship_class = shipclass_habitat_station
							}
						}
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								has_fleet_flag = armada_of_the_voidborn
								has_fleet_flag = star_rider_flotilla
								has_fleet_flag = first_storm_wing
								has_fleet_flag = dwamak_bashers
								has_fleet_flag = unhinged_screamer_flotilla
								has_fleet_flag = frenzied_volunteer_squadron
								has_fleet_flag = her_chosen_champions
								has_fleet_flag = order_of_eternal_night

					is_alliance_fleet = no
					solar_system = {

							is_country = ROOT
						}
					}

							is_same_value = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_01 
							is_same_value = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_02 
							is_same_value = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_03
							is_same_value = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_04
						}

							is_ship_class = shipclass_constructor
							is_ship_class = shipclass_colonizer
							is_ship_class = shipclass_science_ship
							is_ship_class = shipclass_transport
							is_ship_class = shipclass_starbase
							is_ship_class = shipclass_military_special

		save_global_event_target_as = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller

		set_variable = {
			which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_cost_manual
			value = 100
		}
	}
		
	# выбор флота 1
	option = {
		name = ftm_auction.201.fleet_01
		custom_tooltip = ftm_auction.201.fleet_01.tooltip
		trigger = {
			exists = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_01 
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			log = "[Root.GetName] выбрал для аукциона флот 1 ([event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_01.GetFleetName])"
			event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_01 = { 
				save_global_event_target_as = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2
			}
			country_event = { id = ftm_auction.202 }
		}
	}
		
	# выбор флота 2
	option = {
		name = ftm_auction.201.fleet_02
		custom_tooltip = ftm_auction.201.fleet_02.tooltip
		trigger = {
			exists = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_02

	}
		
	# выбор флота 3
	option = {

			remove_global_flag = ftm_auction_lot_2_in_progress

# 2 - ручная настройка стартовой цены аукциона
country_event = {
	id = ftm_auction.202
	title = "ftm_auction.202.title"
	desc = "ftm_auction.202.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_federation_fleet 
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	# -10000
	option = {
		name = ftm_auction.202.minus10000
		custom_tooltip = ftm_auction.202.minus10000.tooltip
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_cost_manual
				value >= 10001
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			change_variable = {
				which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_cost_manual
				value = -10000
			}
			country_event = { id = ftm_auction.202 }
			log = "[event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller.GetName] снижает цену на 10000 единиц. Текущая цена: [Root.ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_cost_manual]"
		}
	}
	
	# -1000
	option = {
		name = ftm_auction.202.minus1000
		custom_tooltip = ftm_auction.202.minus1000.tooltip
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_cost_manual

			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {

		}
	}
	
	# -100

		}
	}
	
	# done
	option = {
		name = ftm_auction.202.done
		custom_tooltip = ftm_auction.202.done.tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			# счетчик текущей цены
			set_variable = {
				which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_cost
				value = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_cost_manual
			}
			# счетчик текущей+100
			set_variable = {
				which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_cost_plus_100
				value = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_cost_manual

				value = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_cost_manual
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_cost_plus_10000
				value = 10000
			}
			country_event = { id = ftm_auction.203 }
			log = "[Root.GetName] выставляет флот [event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2.GetFleetName] на аукцион за стартовую цену: [Root.ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_cost]. Нужно подтверждение"
		}
	}
	
	
	
}





# 3 - запрос подтверждения продажи
country_event = {
	id = ftm_auction.203
	title = "ftm_auction.203.title"
	desc = "ftm_auction.203.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_federation_fleet 
	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2
		
	# подтвердить
	option = {
		name = ftm_auction.203.confirm
		custom_tooltip = ftm_auction.203.confirm.tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			log = "[Root.GetName] подтверждает продажу флота [event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2.GetFleetName] через аукцион"
			country_event = { id = ftm_auction.204 }
			remove_global_flag = ftm_auction_lot_2_in_progress
			set_global_flag = ftm_auction_lot_2_selected
			event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2 = { 
				set_owner = event_target:ftm_auction_country
				set_event_locked = yes
				fleet_event = { id = ftm_auction.299 }
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = ftm_auction_lot_2_time_in_months
				value = 24
			}
		}
	}
		
	# отказаться
	option = {
		name = ftm_auction.203.nope
		hidden_effect = {
			log = "[Root.GetName] выбрал передумал выставлять флот [event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2.GetFleetName] на аукцион"
			remove_global_flag = ftm_auction_lot_2_in_progress	
		}
	}
	
}





# 4 - выставление на аукцион
country_event = {
	id = ftm_auction.204
	hide_window = yes	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
	
		# ОБНУЛЕНИЕ СЧЕТЧИКОВ
		event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
			# корветы (corvette)
			set_variable = {
				which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_corvette_count # всего
				value = 0
			}
			# эсминцы (destroyer)
			set_variable = {
				which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_destroyer_count # всего
				value = 0
			}
			# крейсера (cruiser)
			set_variable = {
				which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_cruiser_count # всего
				value = 0
			}
			# линкоры (battleship)
			set_variable = {
				which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_battleship_count # всего
				value = 0
			}
			# титаны (titan)
			set_variable = {
				which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_titan_count # всего
				value = 0
			}
		}
		
		# ПРИСВОЕНИЕ СЧЕТЧИКОВ		
		
		# корветы (corvette)
		every_owned_ship = {
			limit = {
				ftm_corvette_ship_size_types = yes
				fleet = {
					is_same_value = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2 
				}
			}	
			event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
				change_variable = {
					which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_corvette_count # всего
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
			
		# эсминцы (destroyer)
		every_owned_ship = {
			limit = {
				ftm_destroyer_ship_size_types = yes
				fleet = {
					is_same_value = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2 
				}
			}
			event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
				change_variable = {
					which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_destroyer_count # всего
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
			
		# крейсера (cruiser)
		every_owned_ship = {
			limit = {
				ftm_cruiser_ship_size_types = yes
				fleet = {
					is_same_value = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2 
				}
			}
			event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
				change_variable = {
					which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_cruiser_count # всего
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
			
		# линкоры (battleship)
		every_owned_ship = {
			limit = {
				ftm_battleship_ship_size_types = yes
				fleet = {
					is_same_value = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2 
				}
				
			}
			event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
				change_variable = {
					which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_battleship_count # всего
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
			
		# титаны (titan)
		every_owned_ship = {
			limit = {
				ftm_titan_ship_size_types = yes
				fleet = {
					is_same_value = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2 
				}
			}
			event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = {
				change_variable = {
					which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_titan_count # всего
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# 9 - обратный отсчет счетчика времени лота
event = {
	id = ftm_auction.209
	hide_window = yes	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_global_flag = ftm_auction_lot_2_selected
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
					check_variable = {
						which = ftm_auction_lot_2_time_in_months
						value >= 1
					}
				}
			}
			event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
				change_variable = {
					which = ftm_auction_lot_2_time_in_months
					value = -1
				}
			}
			log = "Лот активен. Осталось месяцев: [event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller.ftm_auction_lot_2_time_in_months]"
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						exists = event_target:ftm_auction_lot_2_max_price
					}
					event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
						check_variable = {
							which = ftm_auction_lot_2_time_in_months
							value < 1
						}
					}
				}
			}
			log = "Лот не был куплен. Возврат флота..."
			event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2 = { 
				set_owner = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller
				set_event_locked = no
			}
			event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
				country_event = { id = ftm_auction.213 }
			}
			remove_global_flag = ftm_auction_lot_2_selected
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					exists = event_target:ftm_auction_lot_2_max_price
					event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
						check_variable = {
							which = ftm_auction_lot_2_time_in_months
							value < 1
						}
					}
				}
			}
			log = "Лот куплен империей [event_target:ftm_auction_lot_2_max_price.GetName]. Передача флота и денег..."
			event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2 = { 
				set_owner = event_target:ftm_auction_lot_2_max_price
				set_event_locked = no
			}
			event_target:ftm_auction_lot_2_max_price = { 
				country_event = { id = ftm_auction.211 }
			}
			event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
				country_event = { id = ftm_auction.212 }
			}
			remove_global_flag = ftm_auction_lot_2_selected	
		}
	}
}

# 12 - сообщение с информацией об успешной продаже флота на аукционе (+ начисление денег продавцу)
country_event = {
	id = ftm_auction.212
	title = "ftm_auction.212.title"
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				ftm_comparible_mods_flags = yes
			}
		}
		text = "ftm_auction.212.desc"
	}
	# mods
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			ftm_comparible_mods_flags = yes
		}
		text = "ftm_auction.212.desc_mod"
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_signing 
	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2
		
	# ок
	option = {
		name = ftm_auction.212.ok
		custom_tooltip = ftm_auction.212.ok.tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			clear_global_event_target = ftm_auction_lot_2_max_price

			# присвоение денег продавцу
				
			event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 							
				set_variable = {
					which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_final_cost
					value = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_cost
				}
			}
			log = "[event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller.GetName]: победила цена в [event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller.ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_cost] энергии. Присвоение денег..."
			while = {
				count = 99
				if = {
					limit = {
						event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
							check_variable = {
								which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_final_cost
								value >= 10000
							}
						}
					}
					add_resource = { energy = 10000 }
					event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
						change_variable = {
							which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_final_cost
							value = -10000
						}
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
							check_variable = {
								which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_final_cost
								value >= 1000
							}
						}
					}
					add_resource = { energy = 1000 }
					event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
						change_variable = {
							which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_final_cost
							value = -1000
						}		
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
							check_variable = {
								which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_final_cost
								value >= 100
							}
						}
					}
					add_resource = { energy = 100 }
					event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
						change_variable = {
							which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_final_cost
							value = -100
						}
					}					
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
							check_variable = {
								which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_final_cost
								value >= 10
							}
						}
					}
					add_resource = { energy = 10 }
					event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
						change_variable = {
							which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_final_cost
							value = -10
						}
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
							check_variable = {
								which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_final_cost
								value >= 1
							}
						}
					}
					add_resource = { energy = 1 }
					event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
						change_variable = {
							which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_final_cost
							value = -1
						}					
					}
				}
				else = {
					#nothing
				}
			}	
			log = "[event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller.GetName]: Присвоение денег завершено"	
		
		}
	}
}

# 70 - ежемесячная проверка наличия флота на аукционе
event = {
	id = ftm_auction.270
	hide_window = yes	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_global_flag = ftm_auction_lot_2_selected
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = ftm_auction_not_can_use_ai_buy
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = ftm_auction_lot_2_selected
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = ftm_ai_buy_block_time
					}
					is_ai = yes
					is_country_type = default
					used_naval_capacity_percent < 0.8
					has_monthly_income = { resource = energy value >= 10 }
					has_monthly_income = { resource = alloys value >= 5 }
					has_communications = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller
					NOT = {
						is_same_value = event_target:ftm_auction_lot_2_max_price
					}
					NOT = {
						is_same_value = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller
					}
					NOT = {
						event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = {
							OR = {
								is_rival = prev
								opinion = {
									who = prev
									value < -50
								}
								their_opinion = {
									who = prev
									value < -50
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				random_list = {
					10 = {
						country_event = { id = ftm_auction.271 days = 1 }
					}
					10 = {
						country_event = { id = ftm_auction.271 days = 4 }
					}
					10 = {
						country_event = { id = ftm_auction.271 days = 7 }
					}
					10 = {
						country_event = { id = ftm_auction.271 days = 10 }
					}
					10 = {
						country_event = { id = ftm_auction.271 days = 13 }
					}
					10 = {
						country_event = { id = ftm_auction.271 days = 16 }
					}
					10 = {
						country_event = { id = ftm_auction.271 days = 19 }
					}
					10 = {
						country_event = { id = ftm_auction.271 days = 22 }
					}
					10 = {
						country_event = { id = ftm_auction.271 days = 25 }
					}
					10 = {
						country_event = { id = ftm_auction.271 days = 28 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}


# 71 - проверка наличия энергокредитов
country_event = {
	id = ftm_auction.271
	hide_window = yes	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_global_flag = ftm_auction_lot_2_selected
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = ftm_ai_buy_block_time
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[Root.GetName]: Запуск скрипта проверки наличия энергокредитов"
		event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
			set_variable = {
				which = ftm_buyer_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_energy_ai_current_count
				value = 0
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			which = ftm_buyer_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_energy_ai_current_count
			value = 0
		}
		save_event_target_as = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_checker
		export_resource_stockpile_to_variable = { resource = energy variable = ftm_buyer_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_energy_ai_current_count }
		event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = {
			set_variable = {
				which = ftm_buyer_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_energy_ai_current_count
				value = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_checker.ftm_buyer_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_energy_ai_current_count
			}
		}
		log = "[Root.GetName]: ЗАВЕРШЕНА ПРОВЕРКА ЭНЕРГИИ ДЛЯ ВХОДА НА АУКЦИОН. КОЛИЧЕСТВО: [event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller.ftm_buyer_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_energy_ai_current_count]."
		
		# проверка наличия энергии для входа на аукцион
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
					check_variable = {
						which = ftm_buyer_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_energy_ai_current_count
						value >= ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_cost_plus_100
					}
				}
			}
			log = "[Root.GetName]: средств для входа на аукцион достаточно."
			country_event = { id = ftm_auction.272 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
					check_variable = {
						which = ftm_buyer_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_energy_ai_current_count
						value < ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_cost_plus_100
					}
				}
			}
			log = "[Root.GetName]: не хватает средств для входа на аукцион."
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = ftm_ai_buy_block_time days = 40 }
		}
	}
}


# 72 - проверка необходимости покупки
country_event = {
	id = ftm_auction.272
	hide_window = yes	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = { # нормальные условия
						OR = {
							AND = {
								event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2 = {
									fleet_power < 2000
								}
								has_monthly_income = { resource = energy value >= 25 }
								has_monthly_income = { resource = alloys value >= 10 }
								event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
									check_variable = {
										which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_cost_plus_100
										value <= 2500
									}
								}
							}
							AND = {
								event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2 = {
									fleet_power >= 2000
									fleet_power < 5000
								}
								has_monthly_income = { resource = energy value >= 40 }
								has_monthly_income = { resource = alloys value >= 20 }
								event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
									check_variable = {
										which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_cost_plus_100
										value <= 4700
									}
								}
							}
							AND = {
								event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2 = {
									fleet_power >= 5000
									fleet_power < 10000
								}
								has_monthly_income = { resource = energy value >= 50 }
								has_monthly_income = { resource = alloys value >= 30 }
								event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
									check_variable = {
										which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_cost_plus_100
										value <= 8600
									}
								}
							}
							AND = {
								event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2 = {
									fleet_power >= 10000
									fleet_power < 25000
								}
								has_monthly_income = { resource = energy value >= 75 }
								has_monthly_income = { resource = alloys value >= 40 }
								event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
									check_variable = {
										which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_cost_plus_100
										value <= 19700
									}
								}
							}
							AND = {
								event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2 = {
									fleet_power >= 25000
									fleet_power < 50000
								}
								has_monthly_income = { resource = energy value >= 100 }
								has_monthly_income = { resource = alloys value >= 50 }
								event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
									check_variable = {
										which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_cost_plus_100
										value <= 35800
									}
								}
							}
							AND = {
								event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2 = {
									fleet_power >= 50000
									fleet_power < 100000
								}
								has_monthly_income = { resource = energy value >= 150 }
								has_monthly_income = { resource = alloys value >= 75 }
								event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
									check_variable = {
										which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_cost_plus_100
										value <= 64300
									}
								}
							}
							AND = {
								event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2 = {
									fleet_power >= 100000
									fleet_power < 250000
								}
								has_monthly_income = { resource = energy value >= 200 }
								has_monthly_income = { resource = alloys value >= 100 }
								event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
									check_variable = {
										which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_cost_plus_100
										value <= 142900
									}
								}
							}
							AND = {
								event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2 = {
									fleet_power >= 250000
								}
								has_monthly_income = { resource = energy value >= 300 }
								has_monthly_income = { resource = alloys value >= 150 }
								event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
									check_variable = {
										which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_cost_plus_100
										value <= 250000
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
					AND = { # угроза - сильный сосед
						OR = {
							AND = {
								is_at_war = no
								any_neighbor_country = {
									is_country_type = default
									OR = {
										is_homicidal = yes
										AND = {
											is_rival = prev
											relative_power = {
												who = prev
												category = fleet
												value >= equivalent
											}
										}
									}
								}
							}
							AND = {
								has_global_flag = gray_goo_crisis_active
								NOT = {
									has_global_flag = graygoo_defeated
								}
							}
							AND = {
								has_global_flag = marauder_crisis_started
								NOT = {
									has_global_flag = great_khan_dead
								}
							}
							has_global_flag = war_in_heaven_ongoing
						}
						OR = {
							AND = {
								event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2 = {
									fleet_power < 2000
								}
								has_monthly_income = { resource = energy value >= 15 }

										value <= 500000
									}
								}

						}
					}
				}
			} # конец проверки
			
			log = "[Root.GetName]: делает ставку на аукционе флота."
						
			#возврат ресурсов при перебивании цены
			
			event_target:ftm_auction_lot_2_max_price = {  
				save_event_target_as = ftm_auction_lot_2_last_price										
				event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
					set_variable = {
						which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_returned_cost
						value = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_cost
					}
				}
				log = "[Root.GetName]: [event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller.ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_returned_cost] energy received, LOT-1 has new owner. Old - [event_target:ftm_auction_lot_2_max_price.GetName]"
				while = {
					count = 99
					if = {
						limit = {
							event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
								check_variable = {
									which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_returned_cost
									value >= 10000
								}
							}
						}
						add_resource = { energy = 10000 }

							}
						}
					}

							event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
								check_variable = {
									which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_returned_cost
									value >= 1000
								}
							}
						}
						add_resource = { energy = 1000 }
						event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
							change_variable = {
								which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_returned_cost
								value = -1000
							}		
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
								check_variable = {
									which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_returned_cost
									value >= 100
								}
							}
						}
						add_resource = { energy = 100 }
						event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
							change_variable = {
								which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_returned_cost
								value = -100
							}
						}					
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
								check_variable = {
									which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_returned_cost
									value >= 10
								}
							}
						}
						add_resource = { energy = 10 }
						event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
							change_variable = {
								which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_returned_cost
								value = -10
							}
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
								check_variable = {
									which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_returned_cost
									value >= 1
								}
							}
						}
						add_resource = { energy = 1 }
						event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
							change_variable = {
								which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_returned_cost
								value = -1
							}					
						}
					}
					else = {
						#nothing
					}
				}			
			}
			event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
				change_variable = {
					which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_cost
					value = 100
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_cost_plus_100
					value = 100
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_cost_plus_1000
					value = 100
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_cost_plus_10000
					value = 100
				}
			}				
			save_global_event_target_as = ftm_auction_lot_2_max_price
			
			
			# снятие ресурсов при установке цены				
		
			event_target:ftm_auction_lot_2_max_price = {

						which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_lot_cost
						value = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_cost
					}
				}
				log = "[Root.GetName]: [event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller.ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_lot_cost] energy is LOT-1 cost"	
				while = {
					count = 99
					if = {
						limit = {
							event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
								check_variable = {
									which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_lot_cost
									value >= 10000
								}
							}
						}
						add_resource = { energy = -10000 }
						event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
							change_variable = {
								which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_lot_cost
								value = -10000
							}
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
								check_variable = {
									which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_lot_cost
									value >= 1000
								}
							}
						}
						add_resource = { energy = -1000 }
						event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
							change_variable = {
								which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_lot_cost
								value = -1000
							}		
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
								check_variable = {
									which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_lot_cost
									value >= 100
								}
							}
						}
						add_resource = { energy = -100 }
						event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
							change_variable = {
								which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_lot_cost
								value = -100
							}
						}					
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
								check_variable = {
									which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_lot_cost
									value >= 10
								}
							}
						}
						add_resource = { energy = -10 }
						event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller = { 
							change_variable = {
								which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_lot_cost
								value = -10
							}
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {

# 80 - ежегодная проверка условий продажи для ии
event = {
	id = ftm_auction.280
	hide_window = yes	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = ftm_auction_lot_2_selected
				has_global_flag = ftm_auction_lot_2_in_progress	
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = ftm_auction_not_can_use_ai_sale
		}
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = crisis_stage_1
				has_global_flag = crisis_stage_2
				has_global_flag = crisis_stage_3
				has_global_flag = crisis_stage_4
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = gray_goo_crisis_active
					NOT = {
						has_global_flag = graygoo_defeated
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = marauder_crisis_started
					NOT = {
						has_global_flag = great_khan_dead
					}
				}
				has_global_flag = war_in_heaven_ongoing
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = ftm_auction_lot_2_selected
						has_global_flag = ftm_auction_lot_2_in_progress	
					}
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = ftm_ai_sell_block_time
					}
					is_homicidal = no
					is_ai = yes
					is_country_type = default
					is_at_war = no
					used_naval_capacity_percent > 0.8
					resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value < 50000 }
					NOT = {
						any_neighbor_country = {
							is_country_type = default
							OR = {
								is_homicidal = yes
								is_rival = prev
								opinion = {
									who = prev
									value < -50
								}
								their_opinion = {
									who = prev
									value < -50
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = ftm_auction_lot_2_num_fleet_count
					value = 0
				}
				every_owned_fleet = {
					limit = {
						fleet_power > 2000
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								is_ship_class = shipclass_constructor
								is_ship_class = shipclass_colonizer
								is_ship_class = shipclass_science_ship
								is_ship_class = shipclass_transport
								is_ship_class = shipclass_starbase
								is_ship_class = shipclass_military_special
								is_ship_class = shipclass_military_station
								is_ship_class = shipclass_mining_station
								is_ship_class = shipclass_research_station
								is_ship_class = shipclass_observation_station
								is_ship_class = shipclass_habitat_station
							}
						}
					}
					owner = {
						change_variable = {
							which = ftm_auction_lot_2_num_fleet_count
							value = 1
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							which = ftm_auction_lot_2_num_fleet_count
							value > 2
						}
					}
					random_list = {
						10 = {
							country_event = { id = ftm_auction.281 days = 5 }
						}
						10 = {
							country_event = { id = ftm_auction.281 days = 35 }
						}
						10 = {
							country_event = { id = ftm_auction.281 days = 65 }
						}
						10 = {
							country_event = { id = ftm_auction.281 days = 95 }
						}
						10 = {
							country_event = { id = ftm_auction.281 days = 125 }
						}
						10 = {
							country_event = { id = ftm_auction.281 days = 155 }
						}
						10 = {
							country_event = { id = ftm_auction.281 days = 185 }
						}
						10 = {
							country_event = { id = ftm_auction.281 days = 215 }
						}
						10 = {
							country_event = { id = ftm_auction.281 days = 245 }
						}
						10 = {
							country_event = { id = ftm_auction.281 days = 275 }
						}
						10 = {
							country_event = { id = ftm_auction.281 days = 305 }
						}
						10 = {
							country_event = { id = ftm_auction.281 days = 335 }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}


# 81 - выставление флота на продажу (ИИ)
country_event = {
	id = ftm_auction.281
	hide_window = yes	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = ftm_auction_lot_2_selected
				has_global_flag = ftm_auction_lot_2_in_progress	
				has_country_flag = ftm_ai_sell_block_time
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		save_global_event_target_as = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_owned_fleet = {
					AND = {
						is_alliance_fleet = no
						solar_system = {
							exists = space_owner
							space_owner = {
								is_same_value = root
							}
						}
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								is_ship_class = shipclass_constructor
								is_ship_class = shipclass_colonizer
								is_ship_class = shipclass_science_ship
								is_ship_class = shipclass_transport
								is_ship_class = shipclass_starbase
								is_ship_class = shipclass_military_special
								is_ship_class = shipclass_military_station
								is_ship_class = shipclass_mining_station
								is_ship_class = shipclass_research_station
								is_ship_class = shipclass_observation_station
								is_ship_class = shipclass_habitat_station
							}
						}
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								has_fleet_flag = armada_of_the_voidborn
								has_fleet_flag = star_rider_flotilla

# 98 - сообщение-уведомление о том что нашу ставку сбили
country_event = {
	id = ftm_auction.298
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		create_message = {
			type = FTM_AUCTION_LOT_LOST
			localization = FTM_AUCTION_LOT_2_PRICE_LOST
			days = 30
			target = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2
			variable = {
				type = name
				localization = COUNTRY
				scope = event_target:ftm_auction_lot_2_max_price
			}
			variable = {
				type = name
				localization = FLEET
				scope = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2
			}
		}
	}		
}



# 99 - сообщение-уведомление
fleet_event = {
	id = ftm_auction.299
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		every_country = {
			limit = { 
				AND = {
					is_country_type = default 
					has_communications = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller
					is_homicidal = no
				}
			}
			create_message = {
				type = FTM_MESSAGE
				localization = FTM_AUCTION_LOT_2_NOTIFICATION
				days = 30
				target = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2
				variable = {
					type = name
					localization = COUNTRY
					scope = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2_seller
				}
				variable = {
					type = name
					localization = FLEET
					scope = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_2
				}
			}
		}
	}		
}
