# 1 - окно выбора флота для аукциона
country_event = {
	id = ftm_auction.301
	title = "ftm_auction.301.title"
	desc = "ftm_auction.301.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_federation_fleet 
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_owned_fleet = {
					AND = {
						NOT = {
							exists = leader
						}
						is_alliance_fleet = no
						solar_system = {
							exists = space_owner
							space_owner = {
								is_country = ROOT
							}
						}
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								is_ship_class = shipclass_constructor
								is_ship_class = shipclass_colonizer
								is_ship_class = shipclass_science_ship
								is_ship_class = shipclass_transport
								is_ship_class = shipclass_starbase
								is_ship_class = shipclass_military_special
								is_ship_class = shipclass_military_station
								is_ship_class = shipclass_mining_station
								is_ship_class = shipclass_research_station
								is_ship_class = shipclass_observation_station
								is_ship_class = shipclass_habitat_station
							}
						}
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								has_fleet_flag = armada_of_the_voidborn
								has_fleet_flag = star_rider_flotilla
								has_fleet_flag = first_storm_wing
								has_fleet_flag = dwamak_bashers
								has_fleet_flag = unhinged_screamer_flotilla
								has_fleet_flag = frenzied_volunteer_squadron
								has_fleet_flag = her_chosen_champions
								has_fleet_flag = order_of_eternal_night
								has_fleet_flag = twilight_congregation
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			random_owned_fleet = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						exists = leader
					}
					is_alliance_fleet = no
					solar_system = {
						exists = space_owner
						space_owner = {
							is_country = ROOT
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							is_ship_class = shipclass_constructor
							is_ship_class = shipclass_colonizer
							is_ship_class = shipclass_science_ship
							is_ship_class = shipclass_transport
							is_ship_class = shipclass_starbase
							is_ship_class = shipclass_military_special
							is_ship_class = shipclass_military_station
							is_ship_class = shipclass_mining_station
							is_ship_class = shipclass_research_station
							is_ship_class = shipclass_observation_station
							is_ship_class = shipclass_habitat_station
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							has_fleet_flag = armada_of_the_voidborn
							has_fleet_flag = star_rider_flotilla
							has_fleet_flag = first_storm_wing
							has_fleet_flag = dwamak_bashers
							has_fleet_flag = unhinged_screamer_flotilla
							has_fleet_flag = frenzied_volunteer_squadron
							has_fleet_flag = her_chosen_champions
							has_fleet_flag = order_of_eternal_night
							has_fleet_flag = twilight_congregation
						}
					}
				}
				save_event_target_as = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_01
				solar_system = {
					space_owner = {
						save_event_target_as = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_01_buyer
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_owned_fleet = {

	# -10000

		name = ftm_auction.302.minus10000
		custom_tooltip = ftm_auction.302.minus10000.tooltip

			check_variable = {

				value >= 10001
			}

		hidden_effect = {

			log = "[event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_seller.GetName] увеличивает цену на 10000 единиц. Текущая цена: [Root.ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_cost_manual]"
		}
	}
	
	# done
	option = {
		name = ftm_auction.302.done
		custom_tooltip = ftm_auction.302.done.tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			# счетчик текущей цены
			set_variable = {
				which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_cost
				value = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_cost_manual
			}
			# счетчик текущей+100
			set_variable = {
				which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_cost_plus_100
				value = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_cost_manual
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_cost_plus_100
				value = 100
			}
			# счетчик текущей+1000
			set_variable = {
				which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_cost_plus_1000
				value = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_cost_manual
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_cost_plus_1000
				value = 1000
			}
			# счетчик текущей+10000
			set_variable = {
				which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_cost_plus_10000
				value = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_cost_manual
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_cost_plus_10000
				value = 10000
			}
			country_event = { id = ftm_auction.303 }
			log = "[Root.GetName] выставляет флот [event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3.GetFleetName] на аукцион за стартовую цену: [Root.ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_cost]. Нужно подтверждение"
		}
	}
	
	
	
}





# 3 - запрос подтверждения продажи
country_event = {
	id = ftm_auction.303
	title = "ftm_auction.303.title"
	desc = "ftm_auction.303.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_federation_fleet 
	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3
		
	# подтвердить
	option = {
		name = ftm_auction.303.confirm
		custom_tooltip = ftm_auction.303.confirm.tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			log = "[Root.GetName] подтверждает продажу флота [event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3.GetFleetName] через аукцион"
			country_event = { id = ftm_auction.304 }
			remove_global_flag = ftm_auction_lot_3_in_progress
			set_global_flag = ftm_auction_lot_3_selected
			event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3 = { 
				set_owner = event_target:ftm_auction_country
				set_event_locked = yes
				fleet_event = { id = ftm_auction.399 }
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = ftm_auction_lot_3_time_in_months
				value = 24
			}
		}
	}
		
	# отказаться
	option = {
		name = ftm_auction.303.nope
		hidden_effect = {
			log = "[Root.GetName] выбрал передумал выставлять флот [event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3.GetFleetName] на аукцион"
			remove_global_flag = ftm_auction_lot_3_in_progress	
		}
	}
	
}





# 4 - выставление на аукцион
country_event = {
	id = ftm_auction.304
	hide_window = yes	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
	
		# ОБНУЛЕНИЕ СЧЕТЧИКОВ
		event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_seller = { 
			# корветы (corvette)
			set_variable = {
				which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_corvette_count # всего
				value = 0
			}
			# эсминцы (destroyer)
			set_variable = {
				which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_destroyer_count # всего
				value = 0
			}
			# крейсера (cruiser)
			set_variable = {
				which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_cruiser_count # всего
				value = 0
			}
			# линкоры (battleship)
			set_variable = {
				which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_battleship_count # всего
				value = 0
			}
			# титаны (titan)
			set_variable = {
				which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_titan_count # всего
				value = 0
			}
		}
		
		# ПРИСВОЕНИЕ СЧЕТЧИКОВ		
		
		# корветы (corvette)
		every_owned_ship = {
			limit = {
				ftm_corvette_ship_size_types = yes
				fleet = {
					is_same_value = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3 
				}
			}	
			event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_seller = { 
				change_variable = {
					which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_corvette_count # всего
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
			
		# эсминцы (destroyer)
		every_owned_ship = {
			limit = {
				ftm_destroyer_ship_size_types = yes
				fleet = {
					is_same_value = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3 
				}
			}
			event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_seller = { 
				change_variable = {
					which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_destroyer_count # всего
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
			
		# крейсера (cruiser)
		every_owned_ship = {
			limit = {
				ftm_cruiser_ship_size_types = yes
				fleet = {
					is_same_value = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3 
				}
			}
			event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_seller = { 
				change_variable = {
					which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_cruiser_count # всего
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
			
		# линкоры (battleship)
		every_owned_ship = {
			limit = {
				ftm_battleship_ship_size_types = yes
				fleet = {
					is_same_value = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3 
				}
				
			}
			event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_seller = { 
				change_variable = {
					which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_battleship_count # всего
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
			
		# титаны (titan)
		every_owned_ship = {
			limit = {
				ftm_titan_ship_size_types = yes
				fleet = {
					is_same_value = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3 
				}
			}
			event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_seller = {
				change_variable = {
					which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_titan_count # всего
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# 9 - обратный отсчет счетчика времени лота
event = {
	id = ftm_auction.309
	hide_window = yes	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_global_flag = ftm_auction_lot_3_selected
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_seller = { 
					check_variable = {
						which = ftm_auction_lot_3_time_in_months
						value >= 1
					}
				}
			}
			event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_seller = { 
				change_variable = {
					which = ftm_auction_lot_3_time_in_months
					value = -1
				}
			}
			log = "Лот активен. Осталось месяцев: [event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_seller.ftm_auction_lot_3_time_in_months]"
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						exists = event_target:ftm_auction_lot_3_max_price
					}
					event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_seller = { 
						check_variable = {
							which = ftm_auction_lot_3_time_in_months
							value < 1
						}
					}
				}
			}
			log = "Лот не был куплен. Возврат флота..."
			event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3 = { 
				set_owner = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_seller
				set_event_locked = no
			}
			event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_seller = { 
				country_event = { id = ftm_auction.313 }
			}
			remove_global_flag = ftm_auction_lot_3_selected
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					exists = event_target:ftm_auction_lot_3_max_price
					event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_seller = { 
						check_variable = {
							which = ftm_auction_lot_3_time_in_months
							value < 1
						}
					}
				}
			}
			log = "Лот куплен империей [event_target:ftm_auction_lot_3_max_price.GetName]. Передача флота и денег..."
			event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3 = { 
				set_owner = event_target:ftm_auction_lot_3_max_price
				set_event_locked = no
			}
			event_target:ftm_auction_lot_3_max_price = { 
				country_event = { id = ftm_auction.311 }
			}
			event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_seller = { 
				country_event = { id = ftm_auction.312 }
			}
			remove_global_flag = ftm_auction_lot_3_selected	
		}
	}
}

# 11 - сообщение с информацией о победе в аукционе
country_event = {
	id = ftm_auction.311
	title = "ftm_auction.311.title"
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				ftm_comparible_mods_flags = yes
			}
		}
		text = "ftm_auction.311.desc"
	}
	# mods
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			ftm_comparible_mods_flags = yes
		}
		text = "ftm_auction.311.desc_mod"
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_signing 
	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = yes
			}
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = ftm_ai_sell_block_time days = 1800 }
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = ftm_ai_buy_block_time days = 450 }
		}
	}
		
	# ок
	option = {
		name = ftm_auction.311.ok
	}
}





# 12 - сообщение с информацией об успешной продаже флота на аукционе (+ начисление денег продавцу)
country_event = {
	id = ftm_auction.312
	title = "ftm_auction.312.title"
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				ftm_comparible_mods_flags = yes
			}
		}
		text = "ftm_auction.312.desc"
	}
	# mods
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			ftm_comparible_mods_flags = yes
		}
		text = "ftm_auction.312.desc_mod"
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_signing 
	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3
		
	# ок
	option = {
		name = ftm_auction.312.ok
		custom_tooltip = ftm_auction.312.ok.tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			clear_global_event_target = ftm_auction_lot_3_max_price

			# присвоение денег продавцу
				
			event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_seller = { 							
				set_variable = {
					which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_final_cost
					value = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_cost
				}
			}
			log = "[event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_seller.GetName]: победила цена в [event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_seller.ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_cost] энергии. Присвоение денег..."
			while = {
				count = 99
				if = {
					limit = {
						event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_seller = { 
							check_variable = {
								which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_final_cost
								value >= 10000
							}
						}
					}
					add_resource = { energy = 10000 }
					event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_seller = { 
						change_variable = {
							which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_final_cost
							value = -10000
						}
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_seller = { 
							check_variable = {
								which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_final_cost
								value >= 1000
							}
						}
					}
					add_resource = { energy = 1000 }
					event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_seller = { 
						change_variable = {
							which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_final_cost
							value = -1000
						}		
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_seller = { 
							check_variable = {
								which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_final_cost
								value >= 100
							}
						}
					}
					add_resource = { energy = 100 }
					event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_seller = { 
						change_variable = {
							which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_final_cost
							value = -100
						}
					}					
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_seller = { 
							check_variable = {
								which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_final_cost
								value >= 10
							}
						}
					}
					add_resource = { energy = 10 }
					event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_seller = { 
						change_variable = {
							which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_final_cost
							value = -10
						}
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_seller = { 
							check_variable = {
								which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_final_cost
								value >= 1
							}
						}
					}
					add_resource = { energy = 1 }
					event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_seller = { 
						change_variable = {
							which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_final_cost
							value = -1
						}					
					}
				}
				else = {
					#nothing
				}
			}	
			log = "[event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_seller.GetName]: Присвоение денег завершено"	
		
		}
	}
}

# 70 - ежемесячная проверка наличия флота на аукционе
event = {
	id = ftm_auction.370
	hide_window = yes	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_global_flag = ftm_auction_lot_3_selected
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = ftm_auction_not_can_use_ai_buy
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = ftm_auction_lot_3_selected
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = ftm_ai_buy_block_time
					}
					is_ai = yes
					is_country_type = default
					used_naval_capacity_percent < 0.8
					has_monthly_income = { resource = energy value >= 10 }
					has_monthly_income = { resource = alloys value >= 5 }
					has_communications = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_seller
					NOT = {
						is_same_value = event_target:ftm_auction_lot_3_max_price
					}
					NOT = {
						is_same_value = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_seller
					}
					NOT = {
						event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_seller = {
							OR = {
								is_rival = prev
								opinion = {
									who = prev
									value < -50
								}
								their_opinion = {
									who = prev
									value < -50
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				random_list = {
					10 = {
						country_event = { id = ftm_auction.371 days = 1 }
					}
					10 = {
						country_event = { id = ftm_auction.371 days = 4 }
					}
					10 = {
						country_event = { id = ftm_auction.371 days = 7 }
					}
					10 = {
						country_event = { id = ftm_auction.371 days = 10 }
					}
					10 = {
						country_event = { id = ftm_auction.371 days = 13 }
					}
					10 = {
						country_event = { id = ftm_auction.371 days = 16 }
					}
					10 = {
						country_event = { id = ftm_auction.371 days = 19 }
					}
					10 = {
						country_event = { id = ftm_auction.371 days = 22 }
					}
					10 = {
						country_event = { id = ftm_auction.371 days = 25 }
					}
					10 = {
						country_event = { id = ftm_auction.371 days = 28 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}


# 71 - проверка наличия энергокредитов
country_event = {
	id = ftm_auction.371
	hide_window = yes	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_global_flag = ftm_auction_lot_3_selected
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = ftm_ai_buy_block_time
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[Root.GetName]: Запуск скрипта проверки наличия энергокредитов"
		event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_seller = { 
			set_variable = {
				which = ftm_buyer_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_energy_ai_current_count
				value = 0
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			which = ftm_buyer_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_energy_ai_current_count
			value = 0
		}
		save_event_target_as = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_checker
		export_resource_stockpile_to_variable = { resource = energy variable = ftm_buyer_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_energy_ai_current_count }
		event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_seller = {
			set_variable = {
				which = ftm_buyer_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_energy_ai_current_count
				value = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_checker.ftm_buyer_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_energy_ai_current_count
			}
		}
		log = "[Root.GetName]: ЗАВЕРШЕНА ПРОВЕРКА ЭНЕРГИИ ДЛЯ ВХОДА НА АУКЦИОН. КОЛИЧЕСТВО: [event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_seller.ftm_buyer_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_energy_ai_current_count]."
		
		# проверка наличия энергии для входа на аукцион
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_seller = { 
					check_variable = {
						which = ftm_buyer_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_energy_ai_current_count
						value >= ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_cost_plus_100
					}
				}
			}
			log = "[Root.GetName]: средств для входа на аукцион достаточно."
			country_event = { id = ftm_auction.372 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_seller = { 
					check_variable = {
						which = ftm_buyer_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_energy_ai_current_count
						value < ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_cost_plus_100
					}
				}
			}
			log = "[Root.GetName]: не хватает средств для входа на аукцион."
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = ftm_ai_buy_block_time days = 40 }
		}
	}
}

						limit = {
							event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_seller = { 
								check_variable = {
									which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_lot_cost
									value >= 1
								}
							}
						}
						add_resource = { energy = -1 }
						event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_seller = { 
							change_variable = {
								which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_lot_cost
								value = -1
							}					
						}
					}
					else = {
						#nothing
					}
				}	
			}
			event_target:ftm_auction_lot_3_last_price = {
				country_event = { id = ftm_auction.398 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = ftm_ai_buy_block_time days = 300 }
		}
	}
}



# 80 - ежегодная проверка условий продажи для ии
event = {
	id = ftm_auction.380
	hide_window = yes	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = ftm_auction_lot_3_selected
				has_global_flag = ftm_auction_lot_3_in_progress	
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = ftm_auction_not_can_use_ai_sale
		}
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = crisis_stage_1
				has_global_flag = crisis_stage_2
				has_global_flag = crisis_stage_3
				has_global_flag = crisis_stage_4
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = gray_goo_crisis_active
					NOT = {
						has_global_flag = graygoo_defeated
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = marauder_crisis_started
					NOT = {
						has_global_flag = great_khan_dead
					}
				}
				has_global_flag = war_in_heaven_ongoing
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = ftm_auction_lot_3_selected
						has_global_flag = ftm_auction_lot_3_in_progress	
					}
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = ftm_ai_sell_block_time
					}
					is_homicidal = no
					is_ai = yes
					is_country_type = default
					is_at_war = no
					used_naval_capacity_percent > 0.8
					resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value < 50000 }
					NOT = {
						any_neighbor_country = {
							is_country_type = default
							OR = {
								is_homicidal = yes
								is_rival = prev
								opinion = {
									who = prev
									value < -50
								}
								their_opinion = {
									who = prev
									value < -50
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = ftm_auction_lot_3_num_fleet_count
					value = 0
				}
				every_owned_fleet = {
					limit = {
						fleet_power > 2000
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								is_ship_class = shipclass_constructor
								is_ship_class = shipclass_colonizer
								is_ship_class = shipclass_science_ship
								is_ship_class = shipclass_transport
								is_ship_class = shipclass_starbase
								is_ship_class = shipclass_military_special
								is_ship_class = shipclass_military_station
								is_ship_class = shipclass_mining_station
								is_ship_class = shipclass_research_station
								is_ship_class = shipclass_observation_station
								is_ship_class = shipclass_habitat_station
							}
						}
					}
					owner = {
						change_variable = {
							which = ftm_auction_lot_3_num_fleet_count
							value = 1
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							which = ftm_auction_lot_3_num_fleet_count
							value > 2
						}
					}
					random_list = {
						10 = {
							country_event = { id = ftm_auction.381 days = 5 }
						}
						10 = {
							country_event = { id = ftm_auction.381 days = 35 }
						}
						10 = {
							country_event = { id = ftm_auction.381 days = 65 }
						}
						10 = {
							country_event = { id = ftm_auction.381 days = 95 }
						}
						10 = {
							country_event = { id = ftm_auction.381 days = 125 }
						}
						10 = {
							country_event = { id = ftm_auction.381 days = 155 }
						}
						10 = {
							country_event = { id = ftm_auction.381 days = 185 }
						}
						10 = {
							country_event = { id = ftm_auction.381 days = 215 }
						}
						10 = {
							country_event = { id = ftm_auction.381 days = 245 }
						}

				value = 24
			}
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = ftm_ai_sell_block_time days = 1800 }
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = ftm_ai_buy_block_time days = 900 }
			event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_seller = {
				# счетчик текущей+100
				set_variable = {
					which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_cost_plus_100
					value = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_cost
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_cost_plus_100
					value = 100
				}
				# счетчик текущей+1000
				set_variable = {
					which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_cost_plus_1000
					value = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_cost
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_cost_plus_1000
					value = 1000
				}
				# счетчик текущей+10000
				set_variable = {
					which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_cost_plus_10000
					value = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_cost
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_cost_plus_10000
					value = 10000
				}
			}
		}
	}
}




# 98 - сообщение-уведомление о том что нашу ставку сбили
country_event = {
	id = ftm_auction.398
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		create_message = {
			type = FTM_AUCTION_LOT_LOST
			localization = FTM_AUCTION_LOT_3_PRICE_LOST
			days = 30
			target = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3
			variable = {
				type = name
				localization = COUNTRY
				scope = event_target:ftm_auction_lot_3_max_price
			}
			variable = {
				type = name
				localization = FLEET
				scope = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3
			}
		}
	}		
}



# 99 - сообщение-уведомление
fleet_event = {
	id = ftm_auction.399
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		every_country = {
			limit = { 
				AND = {
					is_country_type = default 
					has_communications = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_seller
					is_homicidal = no
				}
			}
			create_message = {
				type = FTM_MESSAGE
				localization = FTM_AUCTION_LOT_3_NOTIFICATION
				days = 30
				target = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3
				variable = {
					type = name
					localization = COUNTRY
					scope = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3_seller
				}
				variable = {
					type = name
					localization = FLEET
					scope = event_target:ftm_auctioned_fleet_lot_3
				}
			}
		}
	}		
}




































# 900 - создание империи "аукцион"
event = {
	id = ftm_auction.900
	hide_window = yes	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	
	immediate = {
		create_country = {
			name = "NAME_FTM_AUCTION"
			type = ftm_auction
			flag = {
				icon = {
					category = "special"
					file = "caravaneer_03.dds"
				}
				background = {
					category = "backgrounds"
					file = "00_solid.dds"
				}
				colors = {
					"black"
					"black"
					"null"
					"null"
				}
			}
			effect = {
				set_name = "ftm_auction_country_name"
				set_faction_hostility = { set_friendly = yes }
				save_global_event_target_as = ftm_auction_country
				every_playable_country = {
					establish_communications_no_message = event_target:ftm_auction_country
				}
			}
		}
		log = "АУКЦИОН: СОЗДАН"
	}
}

# 901 - окно дипломатии с Аукционом
country_event = {
	id = ftm_auction.901
	hide_window = yes	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		from = {
			is_country_type = ftm_auction
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		country_event = { id = ftm_auction.999 }
	}
}



# 999 - проверка на геноцидоидальность
country_event = {
	id = ftm_auction.999
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_homicidal = no
			}
			country_event = { id = ftm_auction.9999 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_homicidal = yes
			}
			country_event = { id = ftm_transfer.16 }
		}
	}
}

# 9999 - открытие интерфейса аукциона
country_event = {
	id = ftm_auction.9999
	title = "OK"
	desc = "OK"
	diplomatic = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	custom_gui = ftm_auction_window_gui
	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}
